Jamison Brereton

36 (862)
All Gods
Lu┼Ыa Dh─Бn─Бka
14 verses: jagat─л, except triс╣гс╣нubh 13тАУ14
This hymn is a clear companion piece to the preceding one, X.35. Both hymns con sist of fourteen verses, all jagat─л except the last two in triс╣гс╣нubh. Both have a refrain, and the refrain of X.36 (vss. 2тАУ12) is a minor variant of the last p─Бda of the first verse of X.35. And there is some shared vocabulary. However, X.36 is not tied closely to the morning sacrifice, as X.35 is. The range of gods invoked in X.36 is wider than those in X.35, although there is a distinct ─Аdityan cast here as well (see vss. 1, 3тАУ4, 12тАУ13). The hymn seems somewhat loosely and inattentively constructed.

THERE are the Dawn and Night, the grand and beauteous Pair, Earth, Heaven, and Varuna, Mitra, and Aryaman.
Indra I call, the Maruts, Mountains, and the Floods, Adityas, Heaven and Earth, the Waters, and the Sky.

English translation:

тАЬMay the intelligent and truthful heaven and earth defend us from sin, and from malignant; let not themalevolent Nirс╣Ыti have power over us; we solicit today this protection of the gods.тАЭ

Commentary by S─Бyaс╣Зa: с╣Ъgveda-bh─Бс╣гya

Nirс╣Ыti: mс╣Ыtyudevat─Б, thedivinity of death

Jamison Brereton

Both Heaven and EarthтАФlet those two discerning truthful ones guard us from narrow straits, from harm.
Let Dissolution, bad to meet, not gain mastery over us. тАУ This help of the gods we choose today.

May Dyaus and Prthivi, wise, true to Holy Law, keep us in safety from distress and injury.
Let not malignant Nirrti rule over us. We crave to-day this gracious favour of the Gods.

English translation:

тАЬMay the sounding stone drive away r─Бkс╣гasas, evil dreams, Nirс╣Ыti, and every spirit of ill; may weobtain the happiness of the ─Аdityas and the Maruts; we solicit today this protection of the gods.тАЭ

Jamison Brereton

Let the pressing stone as it speaks drive away demonic forces: the bad dream, dissolution, every devourer.
Might we attain the ─Аdityan shelter and that of the Maruts. тАУ This help of the gods we choose today.

Griffith

May ringing press-stones keep the Raksasas afar, ill dream, and Nirrti, and each voracious fiend.
May the Adityas and the Maruts shelter us. We crave this gracious favour of the Gods to-day.

Geldner

Der t├╢nende Pre├Яstein soll die Unholde abwehren, den b├╢sen Traum, das Verderben, jeden Atrin. Den Schutz der Aditi, der Marut m├╢chten wir erlangen. - Diese Gunst der G├╢tter erbitten wir heute.

Grassmann

Der Pressstein jage t├╢nend die Gespenster fort, den b├╢sen Traum, Verderben, jeden Fresser-Geist; Der Schutz der Maruts und Aditja’s schirme uns, die Gunst der G├╢tter w├╝nschen heute wir herbei.

English translation:

тАЬWe offer the Soma, the protector of the waters, affluent in life, the delighter of the gods, who iswell-praised, the glory of sacrifice, the brilliant-rayed, the vigour which we desire; we solicit today this protectionof the gods.тАЭ

Jamison Brereton

We will bring (forward) the one swollen with the moisture of the waters, providing riches for the living, pursuing the gods, good to invoke, the glory of the ceremony.
Soma, destined for Indra, with his good reins would we hold fast.
тАУ This help of the gods we choose today.

Griffith

We bring the Stay of Life, who makes the waters swell, swift-hearing, Friend of Gods, who waits on sacrifice.
May we control that Power, Soma whose rays are bright. We crave this gracious favour of the Gods to-day.

Geldner

Den von Wasser vollgesogenen, der die Lebenden begl├╝ckt, tragen wir auf, der die G├╢tter einl├дdt, den Gerngerufenen, der das Opfer versch├╢nt; den f├╝r Indra bestimmten Soma wollen wir mit sch├╢nen Z├╝geln lenken. - Diese Gunst der G├╢tter erbitten wir heute.

Grassmann

Den Flutdurchdringer, Lebensschaffer bringen wir, der G├╢tter Lust, des Opfers Schmuck, der schnell uns h├╢rt, Des Indra Soma sch├╢n an Z├╝geln lenken wir, die Gunst der G├╢tter w├╝nschen heute wir herbei.

Elizarenkova

English translation:

English translation:

тАЬWe impolore today the especial protection of the mighty, the great, the irresistible, gods, that we mayobtain riches, and male progeny; we solicit today this protection of the gods.тАЭ

Jamison Brereton

A great thing of the great ones we choose today: the help of the lofty gods without assault,
so that we may attain the good born of heroes. тАУ This help of the gods we choose today.

Griffith

We crave the gracious favour of the Gods to-day, great favour of great Gods, sublime and free from foes,
That we may gain rich treasure sprung from hero sons. We crave this gracious favour of the Gods to-day.

English translation:

тАЬMay we free from sin be in the (enjoyment of the) happiness of the mighty kindled Agni; and in (thekeeping of) Mitra and Varuс╣Зa for our welfare; may we be among the excellent progeny of Savit─Б; we solicittoday this protection of the gods.тАЭ

Jamison Brereton

In the shelter of great Agni while he is being kindled (may we be) blameless to Mitra and Varuс╣Зa for our well-being;
may we be under the best impulsion of Savitar. тАУ This help of the gods we choose today.

Griffith

In great enkindled Agni’s keeping, and, for bliss, free from all sin before Mitra and Varuna.
May we share Savitar’s best animating help. We crave this gracious favour of the Gods to-day.

Geldner

Grassmann

English translation:

тАЬMay Savit─Б on the west, Savit─Б on the east, Savit─Б on the north, Savit─Б on the south, may Savit─Бsend us all desired wealth, may Savit─Б bestow upon us long life.тАЭ

Jamison Brereton

Savitar from behind, Savitar from in front, Savitar from above, Savitar from belowтАФ
let Savitar impel wholeness to us; let Savitar bestow on us a long
lifetime.

Griffith

Savitar, Savitar from cast and westward, Savitar, Savitar from north and southward,
Savitar send us perfect health and comfort, Savitar let our days of life be lengthened!

Geldner

Savitri hinten, Savitri vorn, Savitri oben, Savitri unten, Savitri soll uns Vollkommenheit schicken, Savitri soll uns langes Leben g├╢nnen!

Grassmann

Savitar [sch├╝tze uns] von Westen, Savitar von Osten, Savitar von Norden, Savitar von S├╝den, Savitar schaffe uns Unversehrtheit, Savitar verleihe uns langes Leben.

Elizarenkova
